 " Siddiqui came into the limelight from the films 'gangs of Wasseypur' and 'kahaani'

This question has been asked by the Delhi Police on an RTI filed by Hemant Panda of Odisha by the Central Information Commission, the monitoring agency of transparency in the country
 pandas yah bhi jaananaa chaahate the ki teen bhagodon - gangadhar dahaavatey, surya dev sharma or gangadhar yadav ko giraftaar karne ke liye dilli police ne kya prayaas kiye the? pandas ne ayog se kaha ki vah ek shodhakarta hai or mahatma gandhi kii hatya se jude recordon kaa adhyayan karne ke icchhuk hai
 Mahatma Gandhi was assassinated on 30 January 1948 by Nathuram Godse
 pandas ne kaha ki unhone rashtriya abhilekhaagaar (eneai) ke sangrah main rakhe recordon kaa adhyayan kiya tha, lekin unhen do ahm dastavej nahin mil sake
 These documents were - the final charge sheet prepared by the Delhi Police and the order of action against Godse
 pandas ne teen bindu bataate hue kaha ki unhen inke sandarbh main spashtataa chahie
 These are the points - the three accused absconding in the case and the efforts made to arrest them, the reason for the discharge of the two other accused in the appeal, is not the record of the final charge sheet and the order of action in Godse's case? soochna ayukta shridhar aacharyulu ne kaha ki aaropapatr se jude record darshaate hai ki teen aaropee faraar ho gaye the
 The appellant has mentioned this
 unhone kaha, 'lekin eneai is bare main koi raay yaa soochna nahin de saktaa ki unhen giraftaar kyon nahin kiya gaya tha
 The records show nothing on a primary or final basis
 lekin ek aaropapatr or dastavej hai, jinamein adaalat dwaara tay kiye gaye aaropon kaa zikr miltaa he or inkaa nirikshan apilkarta ne kiya he

 ) The central government has allowed Parvati, the mother of Marhum LTTE chief Prabhakaran, to go to Tamil Nadu for treatment
 haalanki sarkaar ne iske saath kuch sharten bhi rakhi hai
 Giving information on the issue in the state assembly, Chief Minister m Karananidhi said that this decision of the Central Government has been sent to the Indian Mission in Kuala Lumpur by a letter
 parvati vartmaan main malaysia kii rajdhani kualalampur main rah rahi hai
 However, Karananidhi made it clear that this decision of the central government is only for the treatment of 80-year-old Parvati
 vibhinn sharton ke bare main baat karte hue karnanidhi ne kaha ki parvati ko aspataal ke alaava kahin or thaharne kii ijaajat nahin hogi
 If he wants to get treatment in a government hospital, then he is free to do so
 prashasan iske liye uchit prabandh karegaa
 Parvati will not be allowed to meet any political party or banned organization or people associated with it
 vah sirf apane unheen kareebi logon se mil sakengi, jinke bare main unhone pehle se bataa rakhaa he
 Karunanidhi said that the Center ordered a six-month visa to Parvati without interfering with the pending trial in the High Court
 unhone kaha ki aam taur par is tarah kii prakriya main kaaphi vakt lagata he, lekin parvati ke swasthya ko dekhte hue centre or rajya sarkaar ne yah nirnay liya tha ki prakriya ko jald puraa kiya jaae
 Significantly, when Parvati came to Chennai last month in connection with her treatment, immigration authorities sent her back to Malaysia
 parvati ke nirvaasan par kuch raajnneetik dalon ne is mudde ko vidhansabha main uthaaya tha lekin karunanidhi ne unke aagaman ke maamle se sambandhit kisi bhi tarah kii jaankaree hone se inkaar kar diya tha
 On May 30, the Madras High Court gave Parvati two weeks' time to inform the state government if she wanted her treatment in the state
 rajya sarkaar ne kendriya grih mantralay ko is silsile main patr likhakar kuch sharten puri hone par parvati ko rajya main ilaaj kii ijaajat die jane par vichaar karne ko kaha tha
 a 7-year-old child was allegedly unnaturally abused by his cousin on Monday in Ballia district of Uttar Pradesh
 apper police adheekshak kasee goswami ne bataaya ki sikandpur thanashetra ke chakkhaan gaanv main subah saat varshiya ladkaa khel rahaa tha, tabhi chachera bhai parvej (20) use bahala phusalaakar ghar ke peeche sunsaan jagah par le gaya or uske saath aprakritik dushkarm kiya
 Goswami said that Parvez has been arrested after registering a case on the complaint of the child's father

 Union Minister Vijay Goyal has declared the declaration of the Aam Aadmi Party (AAP) as a liar and lit the bonfire of the promises made in the manifestos of Delhi CM Arvind Kejriwal before Holi
 is ghoshnaa patr main sisitivi, wifai , nae aspataal or nae college na kholana or sabase bada anidhikrut colony niyamit na kiye jane or jhuggi jhopadi ko awaas na die jane ke mudde ko shaamil kiya gaya
 Based on pollution and filth spreading in the Yamuna, Goyal has started the Kejriwal bhagao-lok Abhiyan
 kendriya mantri vijay goyal ne kaha ki ham bhi chaahate hai ki dilli ko purna rajya kaa darja mili, lekin jab tak dilli main kejariwal jaisaa araajaktaavaadi mukhyamantri he, tab tak to dilli ko purna rajya kaa darja bilkul nahin diya janaa chahie, kyonki vah apane adhikaron kaa durupyog karenge
 He further said that whoever came to power on the issue of corruption of the Congress is now desperate to form an alliance with the Congress
 goyal ne kaha ki dilli sarkaar ko centre sarkaar va sthaneey nikaayon ke saath milakar kaam karnaa chahie, lekin arvind kejariwal hameshaa takaraav ke mood main rahete hai
 And that is why development works are stalled in Delhi
 unhone kaha ki kejariwal ne jhuthe vigyapanon ke jariye jhuthe vaadon kii jo minar khadi kii he, ham usee kii holi jalaakar logon ko bataaenge ki kejariwal ne jo kaha, use puraa karne ke liye kuch bhi nahin kiya
 The Union Minister believes that the 70 issues of the Kejriwal government on which Kejriwal had issued a manifesto in the last assembly election promised to the people have not been able to fulfill those promises
 jisko aadhaar banaate hue holikaa jalaai gai
 He said that Kejriwal has not yet fulfilled any promise
 unhone pani or bijli mahange hone par bhi kejariwal ko gheraa
 Vijay Goel also surrounded Kejriwal on various issues in 4 years and said that all these 70 points were included in the previous manifesto
 jisamen ek bhi puraa nahin kiya gaya
 He also counted 70 points in which he said, there was talk of 1
5 million cctvs, not a single one was installed
 free wifai nahin diya, nae aspataal or college kya 500 skool bhi nahin khole, udyogon se nikalne vaali dust paf kaa kaam nahi kiya gaya, pradooshan kam karne par koi kaam nahin kiya gaya or dilli ko duniya ko bharat kaa sabase pradooshit jagah pahunchaa diya, jhuggi main do lakh to kya 200 awaas bhi nahin banawaaye, emsidi ko kaam nahin karne diya, jan lokapal bill ko atka diya or ek bhi mohalla sabha nahin banavaaiunhone aage kaha ki puri dilli main ganda pani aa rahaa he, yamuna pradooshit ho rahi he, ek bhi toilet par kaam nahin kiya gaya, dilli main drugs puri dilli main bik rahe hai
 Neither Marshals nor Home Guards were deployed for the security of Delhi, why no policy was made regarding e-rickshaws, why not remove sections 33 and 81 in Delhi's village
 in vaadon kii holikaa jalaane ke peeche goyal kaa mat he ki public dobaaraa in sari ghoshnaa patr ko jaan le jo pichley vidhansabha chunaav ke dauraan kejariwal ne logon se kiya tha
 Goyal claimed that the Aam Aadmi Party will lose the elections in seven seats in Delhi and BJP will win all the seven seats
 gauratlab he ki ne aam aadmi party purna rajya ke mudde ko lekar bijepi kaa 2014 kaa ghoshnaa patr jalaane kii baat kar rahi thi to vahiin iske jawaab main rajyasabha saansad or kendriya mantri vijay goyal jantar mantar par mukhyamantri arvind kejariwal ke vaadon kii holikaa jalaane kii baat kahi
 The formal announcement of the merger of Janata Parivar's parties has not been completed for even a month now that the clouds of crisis are seen on it
 sapa netaa ram gopal yadav ne kaha ki bihar vidhansabha chunaav se pehle yah sambhav nahin he or aisa koi bhi kadam unki apni hi party ke 'deth warrant' par hastakshar karne jaisaa hoga
 However, SP General Secretary Yadav has said that the merger will be postponed for a few days only due to technical reasons
 lekin unki is tippanee par jediu adhyaksh sharad yadav ne tikhi pratikriya vyakt kii or kaha ki vilay pehle hi ho chukaa he
 The SP leader said that it would be best that the LJ Prasad-led RJD and Nitish Kumar's JDU contest the assembly elections this year under the seat sharing arrangement, because if they merge now they will lose their election symbol and the voters Confusion will arise
 sapa netaa ne samvaadadaataaon se kaha, 'vilay taknikiyon kii vajah se bihar vidhansabha chunaav se pehle sambhav nahin he
 If we merge in haste, it will be like signing the death warrant of my own party
 ' The statement of SP leader Ram Gopal Yadav is a clear sign of dissatisfaction in the Mulayam Singh Yadav-led party, because many SP leaders believe that the SP, which has its support base in Uttar Pradesh, is not going to benefit from this merger because Its goal is to unite the mass base of both the JDU and RJD parties in Bihar ahead of the assembly elections due later this year
 janata parivaar se judi raheen partiyon ke vilay kii pichley maheene ghoshnaa hui thi or yah bhi ghoshnaa kii gai thi ki mulaayam nae dal kii aguwai karenge
 It is said that Ram Gopal Yadav has been vocal in his party against the merger of these parties which were associated with the Janata Dal
 janata dal ne 80 ke dashak ke aakhir or 90 ke dashak ke uttarardh main centre main shashan kiya tha
 There is a buzz that JDU president Sharad Yadav will replace him (ram Gopal Yadav) as the leader of the new party in the Rajya Sabha
 ramgopal yadav kii tippaniyon par sharad yadav kii tikhi pratikriya aayi he
 The enthusiastic proponent of the merger, Sharad Yadav, said that Mulayam is authorized to make announcements about the future direction of the new party and the new party has already been formed after the merger of these six parties in a meeting on 15 April
 sharad yadav ne kaha, 'hamaara pehle hi vilay ho chukaa he
 Please ask Mulayam Singh ji, as he has been made the head of the new party and he is the only authorized person to make a statement
 ' Apart from strong opposition in SP against the merger, dissatisfaction is emerging in the RJD and JDU over the delay in seat sharing in Bihar assembly elections and Lalu and Nitish Kumar camped here for three days last week to resolve these issues
 
 lalu or nitish ne aapas main sidhi baatcheet bhi kii or donon mulaayam singh yadav se mili
 Nitish even said that everything is going well
 tippaniyan Many SP leaders believe that their party will not get any benefit from this merger, because JDU and RJD have no base in Uttar Pradesh, on the contrary, SP will suffer loss because it will lose its election symbol and identity for years
 After the hard work of Uttar Pradesh, it has been made among the people of Uttar Pradesh
 pandrah april ko mulaayam, sharad, nitish, lalu or purv pradhanmantri evam jades netaa ech di devegoda samet janata parivaar ke sabhi sheersh netaaon ke sanyukt samvaadadaata sammelan main is vilay kii ghoshnaa kii gai thi
 The names of the new party, election marks, flag and other details were put on a six-member committee comprising Gowda, Lalu, inld's Om Prakash Chautala, sp's Ram Gopal Yadav and Samajwadi Janata Party's Kamal Morarka
 sapa mahasachiv yadav ne haalanki kaha he ki yah takneekee kaarnon se hi vilay kuch din tal jayega
 But JDU President Sharad Yadav reacted sharply to his remarks and said that the merger has already taken place
 sapa netaa ne kaha ki sabase acha hoga ki lalu prasad yadav kii aguwai vaali argedy or nitish kumaar kii jediu is saal hone vaala vidhansabha chunaav siton kii saajhedaari vyavastha ke tahat lade, kyonki agar unhone abhi vilay kiya to ve apana chunaav chihn ganvaa baithenge or votaron main bhram kii sthiti paidaa ho jaaegi
 The SP leader told reporters, "due to merger techniques, Bihar is not possible before the assembly elections
 agar ham hadabadi main vilay karte hai, to yah meri apni party ke deth warrant par hastakshar karne jaisaa hoga
 ' sapa netaa ram gopal yadav kaa bayaan vilay ko lekar mulaayam singh yadav kii aguwai vaali party main asantosh kaa saaf sanket he, kyonki kai sapa netaa maanate hai ki uttar pradesh main apana janaadhar rakhane vaali sapa ko is vilay se koi phayda nahin hone vaala he kyonki iskaa lakshya bihar ke donon dalon jediu or argedy ke janaadhar ko is saal baad main hone vaale vidhansabha chunaav se pehle ekajute karnaa he
 The merger of Janata Parivar-linked parties was announced last month and it was also announced that Mulayam would lead the new party
 bataaya jaataa he ki ram gopal yadav janata dal ke jude rahe in dalon ke vilay ke khilaaf apni party main mukhar rahe hai
 The Janata Dal ruled at the center in the late 80s and late 90s
 aisi charchaa he ki jediu adhyaksh sharad yadav rajyasabha main nai party ke netaa ke rup main unki (ramgopal yadav kii) jagah lenge
 Sharad Yadav's sharp response to Ram Gopal Yadav's comments has come
 is vilay ke utsaahi prastaavak sharad yadav ne kaha ki mulaayam nae dal kii bhavi disha ke bare main ghoshnaaen karne ke liye adhikrut hai or 15 april ko ek baithak main in chah dalon ke vilay ke baad nayi party to pehle hi ban chuki he
 Sharad Yadav said, 'we have already merged
 kripaya, mulaayam singh ji se puuchhie, kyonki unhen nai party kaa pramukh banaaya gaya he or vahi bayaan dene ke liye ekmaatr adhikrut vyakti hai
 ' vilay ke viruddh sapa main kade virodh ke alaava, argedy or jediu main bhi bihar vidhansabha chunaav main siton kii saajhedaari main deree ko lekar asantosh ubhar rahe hai or lalu evam nitish kumaar in muddon ko sulajhane ke liye pichley hafte teen dinon tak yahaan deraa daale rahe
 Lalu and Nitish also had a direct conversation with each other and the two met Mulayam Singh Yadav
 nitish ne yahaan tak kaha ki sab kuch thikthak chal rahaa he
 The comments kai sapa netaa maanate hai ki unki party ko is vilay se koi phayda nahin hoga, kyonki jediu or argedy kaa uttar pradesh main koi aadhaar nahin he, ulte is vilay se sapa ko nuksaan hi hoga kyonki vah apana chunaav chihn evam pahchaan ganvaa baithegi jo saalon kii mehnat ke baad uttar pradesh kii janata ke bich banaayi gai he
 The merger was announced at a joint press conference of all top Janata Parivar leaders including Mulayam, Sharad, Nitish, Lalu and former Prime Minister and JDS leader HD Deve Gowda on 15 April
 nai party ke naam, chunaav chihn, jhanda or anya byore kaa kaam chah sadasyeey ek samiti par daalaa gaya tha jisamen gauda, lalu, inelo ke om prakaash chautaala, sapa ke ramgopal yadav or samaajawaadee janata party ke camel morarka shaamil hai

 They say, "vedanta is definitely Hindu-philosophy, but it is not Hinduism
 sachcha vedanti na hindu hota he, na musalmaan, na buddha yaa christaan( isai), vah keval acha aadmi hota he
 If the ceremonial forms of religion continue to gain importance, then there will never be unity among the religions of the world
 musalmaan kahata rahegaa ki hindu yadi baaje bajaaenge to meri namaaz main baadha padegi or hindu cheekhta rahegaa ki musalmaan yadi gohatya karenge to main apni jaan de duungaa
 Even then, every wise knows that the tomb of religion is not broken by the noise on the road and if a person eats meat, then the responsibility of his sin will not be passed on to another person
 isi buddhi ko man main basaa lenaa or uske anusaar aachan karnaa veydant he
 "comments dinakar hindutv or islamic kattarta par barabari se prahaar karte hai
 It is written that Islam is afraid of being influenced, because Islam, modified or influenced or improved, is not Islam
 udhar hindutv hameshaa is baat kaa abhimaani rahaa he ki hindu hindutv ke bheetar chaahe patit hi samajha jaae, kintu janmana vah sabhi se shreshth he
 The fanaticism of Islam that our prophet is exactly what the prophet had converted and Hindutva's insistence that we have nothing to learn from anyone in the matter of religion, these two walls stand between Islam and Hindutva
 isliye dinakar amir khusro or kabir kaa sahaara lete hai
 The 'four Chapters of Culture' should be recited
 is kitaab se aap kaaphi kuch sikhte hai
 At least you can see the danger of communalism and religious identity politics with a balanced view
 aaj sarkaar badalte hi itihaas lekhan ko maxwadi virodh ke naam par ekatarfa kiya ja rahaa he
 It is singing the glory of a religion or a few castes, they should read 'four chapters of culture'

 But while reading this book, even if you do not agree with many things, you are familiar with Indian culture in a coordinated way
 dinakar bhartiyata ke nirmaan ko hindu paraajay yaa muslim vijay ke chashme se nahin dekhte

 "yadi khusro ko hindustan ne apane adarsh musalmaan ke rup main uchhaala hota to hindustan kii kathinaaiyaan kuch na kuch kam ho jaati hai

 " dinakar samskruti kii is yatra main sampradayikta ke sawaalon se kaaphi jujh rahe hai

 likhte hai ki hindu-muslim ekta ke hamaare desh main teen bade netaa kabir, akbar or mahatma gandhi hue hai

 "dinkar is grappling with questions of communalism in this journey of culture
 wo hal kaa rasta khoj rahe hai

 ek jagah likhte hai ki vah hindu anya hinduon se shreshth he, jo apane dharm ke sivaa islam par bhi shraddha rakhata he or vah musalmaan bhi anya musalamaanon se shreshth he, jo apane mazahab ke sivaa hindu dharm kaa bhi sammaan karata he
 Kabirdas was the incarnation of the rebellion
 veda, varnashram-dharm or jaat-paat kaa virodh unhone usee nirbhikta se kiya jo nirbhikta buddha main dikhaai padi
 He criticized the rituals of Islam with the same bravery that led to the martyrdom of Mansar and, later, Saint Sarmad
 hindu-muslim samasya kaa samaadhaan unhen thik dikhaai padaa tha
 Kabir has passed for five hundred years and even today we think that unless Indian society, Purnarupen, makes Vedanta its base, India will not find any solution to the hindu-muslim problem
 aap soch sakate hai ki sangh parivaar in panktiyon ko padhate hue kitni karavatein badalegaa
 Dinkar looks at Vedanta from a different perspective
 kehete hai, "veydant hindu-darshan zarur he, lekin vah hindutv nahin he
 a true Vedanti is neither a Hindu, nor a Muslim, nor a Buddhist or a Kristan (christian), he is only a good man
 dharm ke aanushthanik rup yadi mahatv pate rahe to vishwa ke dharmon main kabhi ekta nahin ho sakegi

 It is Vedanta to settle this intellect in your mind and to hold it accordingly
 "tippaniyan Dinkar equals Hindutva and Islamic fundamentalism

 There has always been a problem of iphone users that whatsapp is not locked in their smartphone
 android ke liye bhi watsap lock feechar nahin he, lekin play store par darjanon third party eps hai
 Android users lock whatsapp through these apps
 yphone ke liye ye suvidha nahin thi, ap store par bamushkil kuch eps milte hai jo watsap lock karte hai
 But these cannot be assured
 is mushkil ko aasaan karne ke liye watsap ne ab ios yugers ke liye lock feechar laayaa he
 It has been released for all ios users
 agar aap yphone yuj karte hai to ap store se apane watsap ko apadet kar len
 Version 2
 19
 Lock feature has been added to 20
 watsap lock to tareekon se kaam karata he
 Face ID and Touch ID
 phase idi lock ke liye aapke paas iphone X, XS, XS Max or XR main se koi smartphone hona chahie
 Users of iphone with Touch ID can unlock whatsapp with Touch ID
 is nae feechar ko actevet karne ke liye sabase pehle aapako watsap apadet karnaa he
 After this, go to whatsapp settings and select Privacy
 yahaan sabase aakhri main Screen Lock dikhegaa
 Require Face ID / Touch ID will appear as soon as you tap here
 ab yahaan chaar opshans milte hai
 Immediately tops these options and is followed by 1 minute, 15 minutes and 1 hour options
 in opshan kaa matlab ye he ki aap watsap ko kab kitne samay tak bina lock ke rakhana chahenge
 First of all, you will need Face ID or Touch ID to open whatsapp every time you select the option
 jabaki duusare opshan main kuch samay ke baad watsap lock hoga
 According to whatsapp, even if you have locked whatsapp, even if a message appears in the notification, you can reply and read it without unlocking it
 isliye aap is baat kaa dhyaan rakhen
 According to the report, a similar feature is being tested for Android users
 aapako bataa den ki whatsapp bharat main whatsapp Pay kii testing kar chukaa he or ye opshan aapako watsap main dikhegaa bhi
 But this feature has not been officially launched, because right now whatsapp needs clearance from the government

 "we came to know that the IP addresses from which the account was accessed do not fall under our jurisdiction," the official said
